SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\n// Copyright Authors of Cilium\n\npackage policy\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"encoding/json\"\n\n\t\"github.com/sirupsen/logrus\"\n\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields\"\n)\n\n// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions\n// for audit and debugging purposes.\ntype PolicyAuditLogger struct {\n\tlock.Mutex\n\tlogger   *logrus.Logger\n\tlogLevel logrus.Level\n\tenabled  bool\n}\n\n// PolicyDecision represents a policy evaluation decision to be logged\ntype PolicyDecision struct {\n\tIdentity   identity.NumericIdentity `json:\"identity\"`\n\tPolicyName string                   `json:\"policy_name\"`\n\tVerdict    string                   `json:\"verdict\"`\n\tReason     string                   `json:\"reason\"`\n}\n\n// PolicyEvaluationResult represents the result of a policy evaluation\ntype PolicyEvaluationResult struct {\n\tPolicyKey     string `json:\"policy_key\"`\n\tSelected      bool   `json:\"selected\"`\n\tNumIdentities int    `json:\"num_identities\"`\n\tResult        string `json:\"result\"`\n}\n\n// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified logger\n// and log level.\nfunc NewPolicyAuditLogger(logger *logrus.Logger, level logrus.Level) *PolicyAuditLogger {\n\treturn &PolicyAuditLogger{\n\t\tlogger:   logger,\n\t\tlogLevel: level,\n\t\tenabled:  true,\n\t}\n}\n\n// SetLogLevel configures the log level for the audit logger\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"encoding/json\"\n\n\t\"github.com/sirupsen/logrus\"\n\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields\"\n)\n\n// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions\n// for audit and debugging purposes.\ntype PolicyAuditLogger struct {\n\tlock.Mutex\n\tlogger   *logrus.Logger\n\tlogLevel logrus.Level\n\tenabled  bool\n}\n\n// PolicyDecision represents a policy evaluation decision to be logged\ntype PolicyDecision struct {\n\tIdentity   identity.NumericIdentity `json:\"identity\"`\n\tPolicyName string                   `json:\"policy_name\"`\n\tVerdict    string                   `json:\"verdict\"`\n\tReason     string                   `json:\"reason\"`\n}\n\n// PolicyEvaluationResult represents the result of a policy evaluation\ntype PolicyEvaluationResult struct {\n\tPolicyKey     string `json:\"policy_key\"`\n\tSelected      bool   `json:\"selected\"`\n\tNumIdentities int    `json:\"num_identities\"`\n\tResult        string `json:\"result\"`\n}\n\n// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified logger\n// and log level.\nfunc NewPolicyAuditLogger(logger *logrus.Logger, level logrus.Level) *PolicyAuditLogger {\n\treturn &PolicyAuditLogger{\n\t\tlogger:   logger,\n\t\tlogLevel: level,\n\t\tenabled:  true,\n\t}\n}\n\n// SetLogLevel configures the log level for the audit logger\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\tpal.logLevel = level\n}\n\n// SetEnabled controls whether audit logging is enabled\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetEnabled(enabled bool) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\tpal.enabled = enabled\n}\n\n// LogDecision logs a policy decision with the provided identity, policy name,\n// verdict, and reason. This is used for audit purposes to track why specific\n// policy decisions were made.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policyName, verdict, reason string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tif !pal.enabled || !pal.logger.IsLevelEnabled(pal.logLevel) {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tdecision := PolicyDecision{\n\t\tIdentity:   identity,\n\t\tPolicyName: policyName,\n\t\tVerdict:    verdict,\n\t\tReason:     reason,\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity:  identity,\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyKey: policyName,\n\t\t\"verdict\":           verdict,\n\t\t\"reason\":            reason,\n\t\t\"audit_decision\":    json.RawMessage(mustMarshalJSON(decision)),\n\t})\n\n\t// Log the decision in structured format\n\tlogAtLevel(scopedLog, pal.logLevel, \"Policy decision\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs the evaluation of a policy selector against identities\n// in the SelectorCache. This tracks which identities are selected by a policy\n// and the outcome of the evaluation.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey string, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result bool) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tif !pal.enabled || !pal.logger.IsLevelEnabled(pal.logLevel) {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Get the number of selected identities from the cache\n\tnumIdentities := 0\n\tif selectorCache != nil {\n\t\t// Count identities in the selector cache\n\t\tnumIdentities = selectorCache.numIdentities()\n\t}\n\n\tevalResult := PolicyEvaluationResult{\n\t\tPolicyKey:     policyKey,\n\t\tSelected:      result,\n\t\tNumIdentities: numIdentities,\n\t\tResult:        evalResultString(result),\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyKey: policyKey,\n\t\t\"selected\":          result,\n\t\t\"num_identities\":    numIdentities,\n\t\t\"audit_evaluation\":  json.RawMessage(mustMarshalJSON(evalResult)),\n\t})\n\n\t// Log the evaluation result in structured format\n\tlogAtLevel(scopedLog, pal.logLevel, \"Policy evaluation\")\n}\n\n// numIdentities returns the count of identities in the SelectorCache\nfunc (sc *SelectorCache) numIdentities() int {\n\tif sc == nil {\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n\tsc.mutex.RLock()\n\tdefer sc.mutex.RUnlock()\n\treturn len(sc.idCache)\n}\n\n// evalResultString converts a boolean evaluation result to a string representation\nfunc evalResultString(result bool) string {\n\tif result {\n\t\treturn \"selected\"\n\t}\n\treturn \"not_selected\"\n}\n\n// mustMarshalJSON marshals a value to JSON, panicking if marshaling fails.\n// This is appropriate for audit logging where data integrity is critical.\nfunc mustMarshalJSON(v interface{}) []byte {\n\tdata, err := json.Marshal(v)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// This should never happen in practice, but we panic to catch\n\t\t// logic errors during development\n\t\tpanic(\"failed to marshal audit log entry: \" + err.Error())\n\t}\n\treturn data\n}\n\n// logAtLevel logs a message at the specified logrus level\nfunc logAtLevel(entry *logrus.Entry, level logrus.Level, msg string) {\n\tswitch level {\n\tcase logrus.DebugLevel:\n\t\tentry.Debug(msg)\n\tcase logrus.InfoLevel:\n\t\tentry.Info(msg)\n\tcase logrus.WarnLevel:\n\t\tentry.Warn(msg)\n\tcase logrus.ErrorLevel:\n\t\tentry.Error(msg)\n\tcase logrus.FatalLevel:\n\t\tentry.Fatal(msg)\n\tcase logrus.PanicLevel:\n\t\tentry.Panic(msg)\n\tdefault:\n\t\tentry.Info(msg)\n\t}\n}\n","numLines":181,"startLine":1,"totalLines":181}}}
